  <script>
   window.elc_ecom_buid_language_toggle = function(config) {
  function getKeyByValue(object, value) {
    return Object.keys(object).find(key => object[key] === value);
  }

  // take lang from default buid
  var langFromBuid = config.buids[config.businessUnitId] || config.businessUnitId;
 
  if (langFromBuid) {
    var parts = langFromBuid.split("-");
    var proxiedSubdomains = ['fr', 'de', 'nl', 'es', 'pl', 'pt', 'it', 'zh'];
    var subDomain = window.location.hostname.split(".").reverse()[2] || "";
    var proxiedSubdomain = proxiedSubdomains.find(sd => subDomain.indexOf(sd) !== -1);

    if (proxiedSubdomain) {
      parts[0] = proxiedSubdomain;
    }
    var newLang = parts.join("-");
    // get the new buid based on the new lang
    config.businessUnitId = getKeyByValue(config.buids, newLang) || config.businessUnitId;
  }
  delete config.buids;
  return config;
};
  </script>
  <script src="/sites/all/modules/custom/mantle_js/js_boot.js?qqdxbx">
  </script>
  <script>
   JSBoot.pathPrefix = '';
  </script>
  <script>
   var MantleMediaOptions = {"lazy_mp4":true};
  </script>
  <script>
   /*
 * Hook into lazysizes api to lazyload mp4s. Basically since the video
 * starts off preload="none", it doesn't tart loading anything till we start
 * play. We don't lazyload the poster because in reality, you shouldn't need a
 * poster when you're autoplaying.
 */
if (MantleMediaOptions.lazy_mp4) {
  document.addEventListener('lazybeforeunveil', function(e){
    if (e.target.tagName == 'VIDEO') {
      e.preventDefault();
      var video = e.target;
      var playPromise = video.play();
      if (playPromise !== undefined) {
        playPromise.catch(function(error) {
          // due to chrome race conditions. sometimes this can fail
          // if we're trying to play too early
          window.setTimeout(function() {
            video.play();
          }, 500);
        });
      }
    }
  });
}

/*
 * Helper func to unify fixing mp4s in carousels.
 *
 * Notes:
 * We target only videos that have been lazyloaded. so we're still subservient
 * to the lazysizes lazy loading logic.
 */
function _mantle_media_fix_video_carousel($carousel, slideSelector) {
  if (!slideSelector) {
    slideSelector = 'div';
  }
  // this assumes the func is called before
  // slick is initialized.
  // we attach index so we can target slide + clone
  var $slides = $carousel.find('> ' + slideSelector);
  $slides.each(function(i, obj) {
    var $slide = $(obj);
    $slide.addClass('mantle-media-slide-id-' + i);
  });

  $carousel.on('init', function(event, slick, currentSlide) {
    $carousel.find('.slick-active').find('video.lazyloaded').each(function(i, obj) {
      obj.play();
    });
  });

  $carousel.on('beforeChange', function(event, slick, currentSlide, nextSlide) {
    var $currentSlides = $carousel.find('.mantle-media-slide-id-' + currentSlide);
    $currentSlides.find('video').each(function(i, obj) {
      obj.pause();
    });

    var $nextSlides = $carousel.find('.mantle-media-slide-id-' + nextSlide);
    $nextSlides.find('video').each(function(i, obj) {
      var $video = $(obj);
      // sometimes a clone won't have been lazyloaded since it was out of
      // viewport
      if ($video.hasClass('lazyload')) {
        lazySizes.loader.unveil(obj);
      }
      // for now we reset to 0 each time we're about to show again.
      // this syncs the cloned and regular slide
      obj.currentTime = 0;
      obj.play();
    });
  });
}
  </script>

      <div class="split-width-image-text-tout__body content-block__line"><div class="custom-text  mantle-custom-text format--default body-text">
   <p><strong>Skin Concerns</strong><br>
	· Dryness<br>
	· Dullness</p>
<p><strong>What You’ll See On The Ingredient List</strong><br>
	Aloe Barbadensis Leaf Water, Aloe Barbadensis Leaf Extract, Aloe Barbadensis Leaf Polysaccharides</p>
<p><strong>Why Your Skin Needs It</strong><br>
	All skin types can benefit from aloe vera. It is known to have soothing properties and to help your skin retain water. Well hydrated skin is supple and glowing.</p>
<p><strong>The Clinique Expertise</strong><br>
	Our scientists have harnessed the hydration-related powers of aloe vera in multiple ways. One key aloe-based ingredient: activated aloe water. Pure water is infused with aloe barbadensis leaf extract, then supercharged to hold both positive and negative ionic charges, which increases your skin’s affinity to water. We often combine it with other powerhouse hydrators, like <a href="/ingredients/hyaluronic-acid">hyaluronic acid</a>, for effective, deep hydration. <a href="/product/1683/64270/skin-care/eye-care/moisture-surge-eyetm-96-hour-hydro-filler-concentrate">Moisture Surge Eye™ 96-Hour Hydro-Filler Concentrate</a> instantly floods the delicate eye area with crease-plumping hydration.</p>
<p><strong>What Our Clinique Derm Says</strong><br>
	“Activated aloe water is incredible at helping your skin lock in maximum moisture,” says Dr. Sueng Hoon Kang, a board-certified dermatologist based in Seoul, South Korea.</p>
